That office now has jurisdiction over your case. We sent you a notice that explains why we moved your case. Please follow the instructions in the notice. If you do not receive your notice by February 16, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

On January 17, 2023, we denied your request for expedited processing of your I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number SRC2290121940. We do not believe, based on a review of your request, that your case meets one or more of the expedite criteria and otherwise merits expedited processing. We review all expedite requests on a case-by-case basis, and we grant them at the discretion of the director. Information regarding the USCIS expedite policy, including the expedite criteria, is available at www.uscis.gov/forms/expedite-criteria. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
